---
layout: lexeme
lexeme: Aallonharja
---

###  Aallonharja₁

* _This rare proper noun overlaps more common noun *aallonharja* (wavetip)_
* UPOS:  PROPN
* in KOTUS dictionary under:  9
* Origins: finer 
* Possible NER class:  LAST
* Blacklisted:  PROPN-BLOCKING
